Official Gazette of the Republic of the Philippines

The Official Gazette is the official journal of the Republic of the Philippines. Edited at the Office of the President of the Philippines Under Commonwealth Act No. 638

Proclamation No. 338, s. 1938

Signed on October 24, 1938

MALACAÑAN PALACE
MANILA

BY THE PRESIDENT OF THE PHILIPPINES

PROCLAMATION NO. 338

ESTABLISHING AS NORTHERN ILOCOS NORTE FOREST RESERVE FOR FOREST PROTECTION AND TIMBER PRODUCTION THE PARCELS OF PUBLIC DOMAIN SITUATED IN THE MUNICIPALITIES OF BANGUI, BURGOS, LAOAG, PASUQUIN, PIDDIG, AND VINTAR, PROVINCE OF ILOCOS NORTE, ISLAND OF LUZON.

Upon the recommendation of the Director of Forestry, approved by the Secretary of Agriculture and Commerce pursuant to the provisions of section eighteen hundred twenty-six of Act Numbered Twenty-seven hundred and eleven, known as the Revised Administrative Code, I, Manuel L. Quezon, President of the Philippines, hereby establish for forest protection and timber production the “Northern Ilocos Norte Forest Reserve” and place it under the administration and control of the Bureau of Forestry, which shall have the authority to regulate the use and occupancy of this reserve, and the cutting, collection, and removal of timber and other forest products therein in accordance with the Forest Law and Regulations.

I, therefore, withdraw from entry, sale, or settlement, and hereby declare and proclaim to be the Northern Ilocos Norte Forest Reserve, subject to private rights, if any there be, that portion of the public domain situated in the municipalities of Bangui, Burgos, Laoag, Pasuquin, Piddig, and Vintar, Province of Ilocos Norte, Island of Luzon, and described in the Bureau of Forestry map No. F. R. 85, to wit:

Z. 1268/50, identical to corner 4, project 15, alienable and disposable of Piddig, Ilocos Norte; and thence N. 35° W., 425 meters to corner 1, the point of beginning.

Corners 1 and 84 to 87 were marked with the official marking hatchet No. B. F. 355; corners 6, 64 to 68, and 70 to 83, with No. B. F. 473; corner 10 to 27, with No. B. F. 150; and corners 28 to 63, and 69, with No. B. F. 29S.

Containing an area of approximately 15,600 hectares.

This forest reserve contains an aggregate area of approximately 105,242.00 hectares.

In witness whereof, I have hereunto set my hand and caused the seal of the Commonwealth of the Philippines to be affixed.

Done at the City of Manila, this twenty-fourth day of October, in the year of our Lord, nineteen hundred and thirty-eight, and of the Commonwealth of the Philippines, the third.

MANUEL L. QUEZON
President of the Philippines

By the President:
JORGE B. VARGAS
Secretary to the President

Source: Presidential Museum and Library
